### Round 4: Spanish Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-05-13*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 6: Canadian Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-06-10*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 8: French Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-07-01*

### Round 10: European Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-07-22*

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 12: Turkish Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-08-26*

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 14: Belgian Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-09-16*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
